or do you only open 1 new buy and 1 sell, because you have a buy open from earlier.

> Hi Almo nice video...just to clarify, when selling you place 2 sells at 0.34 position size and 1 buy at 0.34 position size. > 
> Ignored

Don't think so  
Sell signal---- 1 lot short and .34lot long Stop loss---- close 1 lot short add 1 lot long and .34 lot short Now he is 1.34 lot long and .34 lot short so 1/3 safety hedge is getting out of whack a bit maybe.  
EA anyone?----make quick work out of seeing if viable edge exists. Don't think there would be many signals per trading period so would take long time to test.  
Also with flash crashes becoming more prevalent any system without proper SL is asking for account draining plus house. Even with SL sometimes. 

We are all One. Be present. Be the Observer

Hi  
A/ 1:100  
B/ for this specific account i used almost full leverage(i used to divide my capital to 200pips)  
C/ if my target reached for the original entry i from the start of the trade set the sl to 40+the spread of the specific pair for the insurance trade  
E/ If i see price go against me 50 pips i start to monitor and use alerts 100 pips from the entry price against me.  
  
Cheers  
Al

> [Quoting cfudge](/thread/post/9493665#post9493665 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> Hi Almo nice video...just to clarify, when selling you place 2 sells at 0.34 position size and 1 buy at 0.34 position size. If price goes against you and eventually a buy signal develops you close the two shorts and open 2 more buys at 0.34 and 1 sell at 0.34. or do you only open 1 new buy and 1 sell, because you have a buy open from earlier. chris
> 
> Ignored

ok,i think you little bit confuse ..  
  
let say we got short position , i open one trade 1lot for this short but!,at the same time i open one trade 0.33 as insurance for long  
if in this case price go against me in full conditions as i mentioned what i do is like that  
  
1.close the short position but leave the long one i had from first one i had with the short signal  
2.i open new only one long trade with 1.33 lot and at the same time open as insurance trade 0.4 lot for the short position  
in this case i now have two long trades / one from the lowest price (the insurance i put from the short signal) and one from the signal price   
and have one short trade as insurance that i put from the fresh long signal.  
  
Cheers  
  
Al. 

Dream, believe,fight for it and you will achieve and NEVER EVER GIVE UP!

  * [ Beertje](beertje)

  * | Joined Oct 2011  | Status: Trader | [446 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=198914)

I made an indicator, it can help you to see better. When you change the settings, don't forget, The first CCi (7777) have another rules, like the other four.  
  
Reduce Signals:  
  
When it is true, the indicator will display the next signal only, when the 3 CCi (777,555,1300) was "empty" in the same time.  
  
Ignore Signals:  
  
(it works only when the "Reduce Signals" is true) When it is true, the indicator will not display another signal, within the adjusted number of candles.

Hi Al,  
  
Just put the ea on a chart. It does not matter which one.  
It can even be a pair which is not one of the eight you proposed  
Also timeframe is not important  
It will give you alerts for the 8 pairs you talked before about.  
  
The EA will scan the 8 pairs, and if all conditions met it gives you an alert.  
  
So the EAwill not transfer to other charts.  
The only thing is that if you change pair in the chart with the ea then the smiley of the ea changes.  
To prevent this i have a second chart with a pair changer. See the two added pictures.  
  
Forget the 2 buttons, this is a next step for auto and manual trading.  
I also added the pair changer.  
  
Hope all it clear now.  
  
BR

Perfect, thanks.  
  
Now on every symbol chance your indicator produces an alert. Can you "fix" this? My suggestion:  
  
Declere global vars  

Inserted Code
    
    
    ...
    double a01,a02,a03,a04,a05;
    double Bar_ok;
    string DPA;
    string   previousAlert="";
    datetime previousTime;

And change the alert lines so it only alerts when i==0 and only once per bar.  

Inserted Code
    
    
    if (i<=1 && (Arrow_dn[1] !=EMPTY_VALUE  || Arrow_up[1] !=EMPTY_VALUE))
    {
     DPA = StringConcatenate(Symbol(), " at ", TimeToStr(TimeLocal())," Almo SCS");
       if (previousAlert!=DPA || previousTime!=Time[0])
       {
          previousAlert = DPA;
          previousTime  = Time[0];
           if (AlertsMessage) Alert(DPA);
           if (AlertsEmail) SendMail(StringConcatenate(Symbol(), "Almo_SCS"), DPA);
           if (AlertsSound) PlaySound("alert2.wav");
        }
    }

the rule for the others: long abowe the adjusted level, short below the adjusted level.  
  
The levels are in the indicator (not external parameters now). The same settings like in the original templete.

  * Feb 1, 2017 5:17pm  Feb 1, 2017 5:17pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar355726_3.gif) emonts](emonts)

  * Joined Nov 2013 | Status: Trader | [494 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=355726)

Hi All,  
  
Changed EA into dashboard indicator.  
So put file in indicator folder/directory.  
  
First 3 colums are general info, spread, pips from open and ADR.  
If stoch values are > 90, green color, < 10 red color, else orange.  
  
CCI, you see last two closed bars in colors like template.  
I exchanged CCI colums 1 and 2, to make period ascending  
  
BR

Hi All,  
  
Update of dashboard.  
Found one bug.  
You must know you need software bugs to keep a good consistant relationship with your customers.  
  
Added user pairs.  
You can select for the default pairs or the own defined pairs, not both.  
Pairs must be sepearated by Comma  
  
The dashboard updates its info every minute to save cpu capacity.  
  
BR

Hi,  
  
Yes  
  
The first three rows are just added info.  
If Pips from open > ADR probably the price will not go higher/lower.  
But this is not part of the setup / strategy.  
This basic info i use in DB's.  
  
The calculation of cci and stoch for high periods, take some cpu capacity. So update every minute.  
That is also the reason that at start of the db it takes some time before info is showed.  
  
BR 

It is not important how often you fall down, but how often you get up again

Sorry if i missed this point in your thread.

> Ignored

  
to receive email :  
  
mt4-->tools-->options-->email :  
SMTP server: smtp.gmail.com:587  
SMTP login: your email ex: [almo@gmail.com](mailto:almo@gmail.com)  
SMTP password: generate password for device on gmail panel and set here  
From: [almo@gmail.com](mailto:almo@gmail.com)  
To: [almo@gmail.com](mailto:almo@gmail.com)  
  
  
for receiving message on mobile mt4:  
  
mt4-->tools-->options-->notificatios:  
set your meta quotes ID here . your ID is : open mobile mt4,go to setting-->message , copy your meta quotes ID  
  
  
  
the main problem of this indi is , it sends to many emails almost 80 emails for a entry point,for example GBPUSD when arrow appear , it send 80 emails and dont mention buy or sell happened . also mt4 message neither worked . im trying to use new version that just posted , i hope those problems fixed .

  * [#237](/thread/post/9515180#post9515180 "Post Permalink")

  * Feb 2, 2017 10:11pm  Feb 2, 2017 10:11pm 

  * [ gringoh](gringoh)

  * Joined Aug 2009 | Status: Trader | [116 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=111371)

Hi Guys,  
  
Here come a dashboard EA.  
  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: Al_DB.png
Size: 111 KB](/attachment/image/2169229/thumbnail?d=1486041088)](/attachment/image/2169229?d=1486041088)   

  
  
=============================  
First:  
=============================  
@ Al: Many thanks for sharing this simple strategy with the community, let see if it is consistently profitable in the long run ;-)  
@ Emonts: Many thanks for sharing a first Dashboard ;-) I do not want to compete with your Dashboard here, I was coding a Dashboard EA on my side and I saw that you shared a Dashboard also. I thought I would share it also instead of keeping it for me  
  
=============================  
Dashboard Settings:  
=============================  
  
Dashboard settings are really straight forward. Here is a quick description of the main functions.  
  
This Dashboard comes as an EA so please install it in your MT4 experts directory.  
  
In OOTB (Out Of the Box Settings):  
  
\- During initialisation, the Dashboard will download historical data from your broker to make sure you have enough data to have the correct calculations. If you are using a fresh MT4 installation, it might take a little bite of time the first time you launch the Dashboard.  
  
\- You can place the Dashboard on any timeframe as the settings for the timeframes used for calculation are coded in the EA (inside EA settings).  
  
\- This Dashboard EA can be used as a Dashboard only which generates signals or as an EA as well. In OOTB settings EA mode is turned off.  
  
\- You can changes the list of pairs to display the 28 standards, for this first version I have hardcoded the list of pairs suggested by Al.  
  
\- in the floating results panel, when trades are open you will notice small red crosses, a click on it would close the open orders.  
  
\- In the info panel the dashboard displays:  
The current spread (in Orange if it is higher than the average spread)  
The average Spread  
Today ADR (in Orange if it is higher than the average ADR)  
The average ADR  
  
You have various alert modes available in the Dashboard.  
  
A click on the pair label or on the signal square (when there is a signal) will open the chart of the selected pair, you can specify the template in the DB settings. I am using Al template as default, if you want the template to be opened correctly make sure to install al Indis from post 1.  
  
Dashboard is movable anywhere on your screen.  
01 - Click to select the dashboard (a little square will appear in the top left corner)  
02 - Let shift keyboard button pressed and left mouse clicked and drag and drop the DB where you want.  
03 Unselect the dashboard to make sure display is correct  
  
If you are displaying the 28 standards pairs you have an option to display separators lines to make the informations more visible.  
  
The file comes as a compiled file as I am using some helpers (mqh) to code.  
  
=============================  
EA Settings and filters:  
=============================  
  
You can filter trades with trading hours, settings are really straight forward. Time filter is using LOCAL HOURS (I can see the questions coming already) as specified in settings.  
  
You can also filter trades per sessions.  
The dashboard is using an automatic GMT offset calculation, no need to change sessions time. The DB is using windows OS to get those values, tested on W10 and on my VPS running W server 2012.  
Open sessions are highlighted in colors below the dashboard. You can specify which currency are tradable during each session.  
  
I tried to keep the EA settings as simple as possible, using Al suggestions and trade management, however I have added a couple of options (possibility to place SL and TP with trades, options to use a second leg trade as Al is doing).  
  
In OOTB settings:  
\- all individual SL and TP are on off.  
\- Fixed MM is used First leg with 0.1 lot and second leg with 0.03 lot.  
\- Both legs will be closed if leg 1 reach 40 pips.  
\- Opposite orders will be opened if the dashboard generates an opposite signal.  
\- Spread filter is on (if current spread is higher than average spread the trade is not open), only applicable for the first initial trade to open.  
\- ADR filter is off (if on and today ADR > average ADR or distance between Today ADR and average ADR < inputs in EA settings the trade is not open), only applicable for the first initial trade to open.  
  
Trade are open when a signal is generated on last closed candle. There is an option to use the current open candle instead.  
  
I have not fully tested the trade management so be careful and test it  
  
Working perfectly on MT4 build 1031, windows 10, coded with editor 1498.  
Dashboard tested on TradersWay which has a suffix i and working fine.  
  
Thats it, there might be a few glitches here or there do not hesitate to report them ;-)  
  
=============================  
Additional info:  
=============================  
I have coded the DB as emonts, please note that the first CCI on the Dashboard is the one with the Slowest period (555) when on Al templated the first one (the upper one) is the period 777.  
  
40 pips as TP sounds good for pairs suggested by Al. For other pairs with a lower ADR the TP might have to be lower.  
  
Have fun,  
G

Ok, here is my modified version. I name it Almo_CSC_with_Alert_v1.00**j**.mq4(j for jagg **![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f609.png?v=15.1)**)  
  
* I've added a new setting to **reduce cpu usage** (see picture).  
* I've changed the indicator to look for a **signal at bar -1 (not the actual bar which is forming)**. So it shouldn't be any arrow on that bar which still is forming.  
* There is **only one arrow** shown in the chart **for one direction**. So when we have a buy arrow this buy arrow will be the only buy arrow until we have a counter entry signal (sell arrow).  
  
Please test it!

  * Feb 3, 2017 1:09am  Feb 3, 2017 1:09am 

  * [ gringoh](gringoh)

  * Joined Aug 2009 | Status: Trader | [116 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=111371)

@ Strom: thanks  
@ Al: Results are reported according to the EA Magic Number, if you want to see results of manual trades (without Magic Numbers) you have to input 0 in EA settings. Please also make sure to switch Off autotrading to make sure that the EA do not manage some trades opened manually (to avoid potential issues).  
  
One additional note:  
  
At the moment when trade are open comments are:  
Gig-In Trend Buy (for the in trend trade Leg 1)  
GiG-CTT Sell (for the CTT trade Leg 2)  
  
If opposite trades are open  
GiG-Opposite Buy  
GiG-Opposite Sell  
  
I am considering changing those comments for:  
  
GiG-L1-In Trend Buy  
GiG-L2-CTT Sell  
  
And  
GiG-L1-Opposite Buy  
GiG-L2-Opposite Sell  
  
What do you think guys?

> @ Strom: thanks @ Al: Results are reported according to the EA Magic Number, if you want to see results of manual trades (without Magic Numbers) you have to input 0 in EA settings. Please also make sure to switch Off autotrading to make sure that the EA do not manage some trades opened manually (to avoid potential issues). One additional note: At the moment when trade are open comments are: Gig-In Trend Buy (for the in trend trade Leg 1) GiG-CTT Sell (for the CTT trade Leg 2) If opposite trades are open GiG-Opposite Buy GiG-Opposite Sell I am considering...
> 
> Ignored

if i disable the auto trade i still will get alerts ?

  * [#261](/thread/post/9516485#post9516485 "Post Permalink")

  * Feb 3, 2017 1:47am  Feb 3, 2017 1:47am 

  * [ gringoh](gringoh)

  * Joined Aug 2009 | Status: Trader | [116 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=111371)

@ Strom : Everything is possible but as I stated I tried to keep this Dashboard as simple as possible and to code only Al rules.  
  
I have coded some much more complex Dashboard with a lot of options but at the end when there are too many options it is almost always a failure.  
  
The best way to go from my point of view is to have a Dashboard EA like this one and to use it semi manually. You let the Dashboard open the trade for you (at least if you are not in front of the computer when there is a signal the Dashboard open the trade for you). And then when you are in front of the screen, if you are not comfortable with the trade you can decide to close it manually.  
  
1: In the DB you have a red cross (at the bottom) which allow to close ALL trades, and when some trades are open, on the left of the floating results, some red crosses will appear also, and allow you to close only the pairs trades (please check my previous screenshots you will see them).  
  
2: For the time being I wont code any ADR filter (excepted the one already coded). Best thing is to add or remove pairs from the Dashboard list of pairs. Lets play with this tools first, and once we have some stats we can discuss a potential additional ADR filter.  
  
3: To go further with the ADR filter, we can also imagine a TP according to the pair ADR (the current TP of 40 pips is around 1/3 to the ADR of GBP pairs), so we can imagine to have a dynamic TP of the pairs ADR. But thats for later once we have stats ;-) For SL I have no view at the moment, we only have the opposite signal in the DB at the moment.  
  
Cheers,

Hi Guys,  
  
Here is an update for today. I have fixed a glitch and added the Dynamic ADR TP. Now I think we have a good candidate for a week test starting next week. I am going to set 2 DB on my VPS, 1 to test the pairs recommended by Al with a fix TP of 40 pips, and a second test with the 28 standard pairs with a Dynamic TP of 25 % the average ADR.  
  
================================  
Fixed Glitch  
================================  
Yesterday when I have updated the DB to limit trades to 1 buy in Trend and 1 sell in Trend I have forgotten that when you open a trade according to Al rules you were opening a buy and a sell at the same time, so trading would have been limited to 1 trade in Trend only. Now this version fix this issue and trading is limited to 1 buy and 1 sell in trend with their CTT leg.  
  
================================  
Dynamic ADR  
================================  
As discussed yesterday, I have included a Dynamic ADR TP. This option can be useful to test how the DB performs with the 28 standard pairs. In OOTB setting the % is set at 25 % the average ADR value which is, from my point of view, roughly the TP that Al is using for the recommended pairs. I have also included a minimal and maximal value for this Dynamic ADR TP in order to avoid abnormal value when there is an abnormally low or high average ADR (which occurs from time to time). There is also an option to display those Dynamic ADR TP value on the right side of the DB (as in my previous pic). On default this option is on false to avoid cluttering the DB. You can also see this value if you hover your mouse over the various average ADR values.  
  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: ALADRSETTINGS.png
Size: 30 KB](/attachment/image/2170973/thumbnail?d=1486123042)](/attachment/image/2170973?d=1486123042)   

  
  
================================  
Session filter  
================================  
Here is a quick note for guys who want to test the session currency filter. The dashboard is using an automatic GMT offset calculation to see which sessions are open or not. Based on that some pairs are allowed for trading or not. In the screenshot below, you can note that only London session is open (Green color). In the DB settings, you can note that during London session only EUR, CHF and GBP currencies are allowed for trading (you can note that those currencies are in Green below sessions time on the DB). The result would be that only pairs which have one of those currencies in the base or quote would be allowed for trading.  
  
Those settings in the DB are the most common ones which make sense. However, from my point of view this session currency filter would be more useful during Asia session than during London and NY sessions, which mean you would probably want to allow all currencies for trading during London and NY sessions.  
  

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

[![Click to Enlarge

Name: ALSESSIONS.png
Size: 118 KB](/attachment/image/2170974/thumbnail?d=1486123043)](/attachment/image/2170974?d=1486123043)   

  
  
================================  
Technical note  
================================  
In the dashboard, the signals are checked this way:  
  
If the previous closed bar has a signal and the bar before do not have a signal, then this is a valid signal and it is highlighted in Red or Lime on the DB.  
  
If the previous closed bar has a signal and the bar before has a signal, then this is a continuation signal (not a valid signal to enter a trade) and it is highlighted in Teal or Pink.  
  
The dashboard is not checking for the first signal of the day (for CPU issue). If your dashboard is running 24/24 a day, as the dashboard is limiting trading to 1 in trend buy and 1 in trend sell a day only the first valid signals would trigger a trade. It also means that if your guys are launching the DB in the middle of the day the DB might trigger a trade with a signal which is not the first signal of the day.  
  
Hope it make sense.  
  
Only 1 DB option was not tested yet as I didnt had a setup to test it yet, the opposite signal trade.  
  
================================  
Additional filter  
================================  
As I said above I think this DB is ready for a forward test. I dont plan to add any other options for the moment as we have already all Als rules coded and even more.  
  
From my experience, all Dashboards monster with tons of options are always failure, so lets try to keep it simple.  
  
Off course we are people with an open mind here and any suggestions are welcome, and off course if Al has other ideas I will update the DB ;-)  
  
================================  
My settings for my test  
================================  
You can also find attached in this post my 2 sets files.  
  
1st set file: Pairs recommended by Al with a fix TP of 40 pips.  
2nd set file: 28 standard pairs with a Dynamic TP of 25 % the average ADR.  
  
I am also using a time filter from "+8.00,-17.00" (my local time) which is from Frankfurt open until London Close.  
  
PS: you can note that there is a small clock at the bottom of the dashboard below the Pairs labels, if the clock is green trading time is on, if the clock is red trading time is off.  
  
Cheers,  
G

@ corsican :  
  
\- Yep stealth TP close both legs trades.  
  
\- Opposite signal should (example for a in Trend buy with an opposite signal)  
  
==> close the BUY initial Leg 1 in trend order  
==> let the SELL initial Leg 2 CTT order open  
==> Open a Leg 1 SELL order  
==> Open a Leg 2 CTT buy order  
  
The DB should work as intended by I didnt had such a setup yet to test it. I will report once I have a confirmation.

Trade limitation is only for initial signals.  
  
Opposite trades mode is a different story it open an opposite trade when a trade is already open and you have an opposite signal.  
  
There is no limitation in number of trades for this one for the moment as you shouldn't have more than 2 opposite signal a day.

When the EA is offline (if your MT4 platform is not connected): then nothing happen.  
  
Concerning the trading time filter, it is applicable only for the initial trade, for opposite signals, they can be triggered any time (that's how it works at the moment).

Hey guys  
  
First and foremost a great big thanks to Almo and Gringoh for their amazing work on this project as well as all the others who have contributed including emonts and jagg  
  
Just thought i'd share my results so far with the default settings with one change, my tp is 20 pips as you can see, with a stop loss of 30. not a good ratio according to most i know, but the results speak for themself  
  
I'm gutted i cant show todays results as it was looking rather spectacular at about 23%! I then refreshed a setting and todays results are nowhere to be seen...lol  
  
I've played around with this project quite a bit so far, excluding certain CCI's, using different time frames and thus far found the dafault settings and timeframe of 1m the best.  
  
I'm certainly finding the CHF pairs quite an annoyance but i would like to see this week out before removing any pairs  
  
My only concern is the NEWS. The only thing this wicked machine lacks in my opinion is an easy filter to filter those pairs that are going to be affected by news. if this could be added in future, would be a great help!  
  
Anyways, I'll keep you guys updated.

#  [](/thread/635469-csc-method-ccistochasticcombo-almo-version-and-methodology)CSC Method (Cci,Stochastic,Combo) Almo Version and methodology

  * [#341](/thread/post/9538608#post9538608 "Post Permalink")

  * Edited 9:29pm  Feb 8, 2017 9:17pm | Edited 9:29pm 

  * [ gringoh](gringoh)

  * Joined Aug 2009 | Status: Trader | [116 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=111371)

Here is a quick DB and results update:  
  
=========================  
Modifications  
=========================  
\- Now, the pip count for all displayed results is showing only the L1 orders pip count (the previous DB was showing the net of both legs orders and was a bite messy). The total is displayed also.  
  
\- I have also included an additional information to show a Win/Loss counter per pair and for the total.  
  
\- I have included some buttons just after the pairs label. Green = trading on, red off for Buy/Sell. On init there are turned ON by default, you can switch all buttons status with the 2 buttons at the bottom. Those buttons are filtering only the initial trades as the other filters.  
  
PS: Buttons not tested yet but should work as intended as I have already used those filters in other DB.  
  
=========================  
Note  
=========================  
I wont include any news filter in the DB. I did that in the past and it is always a nightmare as you rely on website informations and formatting and for any reason if something change the function wont work anymore.  
  
You have various functions which can help you to avoid trading during news: Trading hour filter, Session filter, now the buttons to allow buy or sell.  
  
=========================  
Results update  
=========================

  * Feb 8, 2017 10:11pm  Feb 8, 2017 10:11pm 

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar23218_2.gif) Jagg](jagg)

  * Joined Oct 2006 | Status: Trader | [533 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=23218)

> [Quoting tradur](/thread/post/9519252#post9519252 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> {quote} @Jagg: Is it possible to make a target Arrow/line according to the ADR in the dashboard?
> 
> Ignored

Ok, here is a new version of the indicator _(Almo_CSC_with_Alert_v1.0**2** j.mq4)_  
  
***added*** Show ADR value(s) on a corner of your choice  
***added*** Show trade history - this shows if past arrows were winners or loosers (according to your set tp/sl)  
(green line from entry to tp if it was a winner, red line from entry to sl if it was a looser - or a line from entry to next arrow if neither tp or sl reached)  
***added*** Show TP/SL line(s) on an active signal (this is for information only - no trade is executed if it's reached)  
  
_Please test it on a live market. I didn't had any new signal so "show tp/sl lines" is untested if it works as designed._  
  
**I've added also my used template. I added buttons for easy symbol change (with Almos default pairs) and replaced the pivot indicator.**

Hello,  
  
I have noticed that already when trades are lining up, some go wrong. I think it has to do with the CCI 7777 setting. If you check the history and you only take the first signal after the CCI 7777 changed than the chances of a good trade increase. If the EA takes signals after that first Signal, the likelyhood for a win is not that great. Just do a visual check, you will see.  
  
@ gringoh. Would it be possible for the EA to only trade the first Signal after the CCI 7777 changed and ignore all the signals that come after until the CCI 7777 changes again?  
  
Thx.  
D.

i got to watch the video for a bit before it went private, so here is my explanation:  
  
on GBPAUD we would enter normally like the system says with the blue arrow, unfortunately the price reverses and starts going lower. now comes the reverse trade (green line on the chart), we would close the initial position with around 65 loss, and open new trade in new direction.  
  
IF we wait for the normal reverse signal, the loss would be 130 pips (red line and arrow represents the old reverse trade)

> [Quoting carelkersna](/thread/post/9559705#post9559705 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> {quote} i got to watch the video for a bit before it went private, so here is my explanation: on GBPAUD we would enter normally like the system says with the blue arrow, unfortunately the price reverses and starts going lower. now comes the reverse trade (green line on the chart), we would close the initial position with around 65 loss, and open new trade in new direction. IF we wait for the normal reverse signal, the loss would be 130 pips (red line and arrow represents the old reverse trade) {image}
> 
> Ignored

Thanks for the explanation, do you have the indications about this new signal (the detailled calculation), it would help to code it into the DB EA.  
  
Cheers,  
G

i, unfortunately dont have any exact calculations about this reverse signal indicator, however i do have a hunch of how it works  
  
BUY SIGNAL:  
CCI 555 > 155  
CCI 1333 > 155  
CCI 2333 > 0  
EMA200 **ABOVE** EMA365  
  
SELL SIGNAL:  
CCI 555 < 155  
CCI 1333 < 155  
CCI 2333 < 0  
EMA200 **BELOW** EMA365  
  
  
BUT this indicator can also give false signals, see images below  
from YELLOW(original entry) to RED(new reverse signal) is about 32 pips  
from RED(new reverse entry) to GREEN(original reverse signal) is about 40 pips  
so in total it would generate a 72 pip DD, not sure how frequent this is tho, hopefully not very frequent ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar435053_2.gif) sevan62](sevan62)

  * Joined Nov 2015 | Status: Coder | [510 Posts](/search?do=process&provider=Member&searchuser=435053)

Hi fellow traders.  
I was interested in this simple strategy which seemed to be powerfull and developed EA by Almo CSC rules in order to back test it and maybe use in trading. Unfortunately almost all currency pairs showed losing results in back-tests. Back-tests were run:

  1. In Open prices model as EA operates with M1 bar open prices. This method reduces testing time while the results are the same comparing with all ticks method.
  2. Using deep 2+ years M1 history to get more deals under different market conditions.
  3. Default EA setting match Almo CSC basic strategy rules although you may change EA inputs and try to get better results.

Sorry but at the moment I do not see any market advantage in this strategy.  
You may download back-test results and EA, run back-taest yourself and compare with mine.  
EA doesn't need any external indicator or anything else to work in MT terminal/tester.  
In oreder to be sure that EA back-tests are true you may run it 1 week on demo account and then run the same period in MT4 tester back-test and comare results. They match 99%.  
To be honest this strategy realy showed good results in January 2017 according to back-tests that is why Almo's gain is likly caused by luck but I can not see any winning agde in long term.  
Hope to prevent you from wasting time and maybe money. ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f60a.png?v=15.1)  
Take care and stay green.

  * [![](https://assets.faireconomy.media/nfs/customavatars/thumbs/medium/avatar435053_2.gif) sevan62](sevan62)

> [Quoting Jagg](/thread/post/9569439#post9569439 "View Quoted Post")
> 
> Disliked
> 
> {quote} Interesting results, thanks! But do you have Trade1 and Trade2 in your EA (e.g. for a buy 0.10 lot long + 0.3 lot short and so on?! Only one trade per day or max 2 when we reach counter signal and so on ....)
> 
> Ignored

Yes EA places **one trade per day**. Opposite trade may be opened at the same day if it is allowed by EA settings.  
My EA do not have "**insurence opposite order** " according to Almo original strategy as it doesn't bring any trading advantage. Say you open Buy 1.0 lot and Sell 0.3 lot at the same time. And having reversal signal you close the main order 1.0 lot and remain "insurance" 0.3 order. This point is absolutely equal that you have opened Buy 0.7 from the very begining and closed it at the checkpoint. You may open or not reversal order at this checkpoint but it doesn't cause much difference in average performance. You may test it yourself as EA has 3 differen types of close opportinities of losing trade:

  1. Close losing trade according to SL,
  2. Close losing trade according to opposite singal without opening reversal order,
  3. Close losing trade according to opposite singal with opening reversal order,

"Insurance" 0.3 lot reverse order causes loss only:

  1. Increasing spread loss for opening & closing 0.3 lot.
  2. Increasing swap loss in case trade lasting more than 1 day.

It is as simple as arithmetic: **1.0 - 0.3 = 0.7**  
  

> [Quoting Jagg](/thread/post/9569439#post9569439 "View Quoted Post")

Imho code must be as short as possible while controlling all necessary trading events and executing orders. The strategy is too simple so there is no need to complicate algorithm and code. You may check yourself if EA obey the rules. I've alredy checked myself. ![](https://resources.faireconomy.media/images/emojis/64/1f609.png?v=15.1)

Hi Guys,  
  
I was busy with personal work and so I didnt have much time to work on the DB EA so far, but a major update is coming in a few minutes.  
  
I can see that some of you have some great results.  
  
And I can see that some of you still do not have signals with the latest DB EA version available in this thread (due to CCI 5 which do not have values). Initially, I thought it was due to historical data missing but there might be another reason. I had some issues with some of my tools with MT Crap latest build (1045) which was buggy. I had to force the update to the latest BETA build 1049 and it seems that those issues are fixed now (my other tools which were not working anymore with build 1045 are now working fine again as they always were). I give more explanations to update to beta build 1049 here: [http://www.greed-is-good.com/forum/v...php?p=540#p540](http://www.greed-is-good.com/forum/viewtopic.php?p=540#p540)  
  
As you have probably already noted, Al has decided to close this thread for non-activity reason (post 1).  
  
Considering the new features in the next DB EA update I will open a new thread for it. Thats what not my plan to open a thread for it, but you will understand why when you will see it.  
  
The new DB EA will come in a few minutes, the time to prepare the wording for it, stay tuned, I will post a link in this thread once ready.  
  
Cheers,  
G
